function Trig_Vote_start_Func011Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Vote_start_Func011Func001Func003C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

function Trig_Vote_start_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_voting_procedure = true
    call PolledWait( 2.00 )
    call DialogSetMessageBJ( udg_vote, "TRIGSTR_3732" )
    call DialogAddButtonBJ( udg_vote, "TRIGSTR_3878" )
    set udg_allyvote[0] = GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ( udg_vote, "TRIGSTR_3733" )
    set udg_allyvote[1] = GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    call DialogAddButtonBJ( udg_vote, "TRIGSTR_3734" )
    set udg_allyvote[2] = GetLastCreatedButtonBJ()
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Vote_start_Func011Func001C() ) then
            call DialogDisplayBJ( true, udg_vote, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()) )
        else
            call DoNothing(  )
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

            set udg_STATE[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 2

            call DialogDisplayBJ( true, udg_DAILOG_2, GetTriggerPlayer() )
        else

                set udg_STATE[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 3
                call DialogSetMessageBJ( udg_DAILOG_2, "TRIGSTR_3055" )
                call DialogDisplayBJ( true, udg_DAILOG_2, GetTriggerPlayer() )
            else
                if ( Trig_Dialog_Click_NA_Func001Func004Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_STATE[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 4
                    call DialogSetMessageBJ( udg_DAILOG_2, "TRIGSTR_3344" )
                    call DialogDisplayBJ( true, udg_DAILOG_2, GetTriggerPlayer() )
                else
                    if ( Trig_Dialog_Click_NA_Func001Func004Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_STATE[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 5
                        call DialogSetMessageBJ( udg_DAILOG_2, "TRIGSTR_3883" )

                        if ( Trig_Dialog_Click_NA_Func001Func004Func001Func001Func001Func004C() ) then
                            set udg_ALLYSETTING[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = false

function Trig_Dip_War_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func003001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) + "???|cffff0000?|r?????. 2?????????." ) )
                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func004001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + " |cffff0000?|r?????. 2??????????" ) )
                set udg_WARTOPLAYER[0] = GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())
                set udg_WARTOPLAYER[1] = GetForLoopIndexA()
                set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) ) + ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) )] = true
                set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) ) + ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) )] = true
                call TriggerExecute( gg_trg_War_Timer )
            else
                if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func003001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) + "???|cffff0000?|r?????. 2?????????." ) )
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func004001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + " |cffff0000?|r?????. 2??????????" ) )
                    set udg_WARTOPLAYER[0] = GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())
                    set udg_WARTOPLAYER[1] = GetForLoopIndexA()
                    set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) ) + ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) )] = true
                    set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) ) + ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) )] = true
                    call TriggerExecute( gg_trg_War_Timer )
                    call TriggerSleepAction( 270.00 )
                    set udg_PlayerAllyT[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = false
                    set udg_PlayerAllyT[GetConvertedPlayerId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()))] = false
                else
                    if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func002001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) + "???|cffff0000?|r?????. 2?????????." ) )
                        call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func003001001)), ( ( "          " + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + " |cffff0000?|r?????. 2??????????" ) )
                        set udg_WARTOPLAYER[0] = GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())
                        set udg_WARTOPLAYER[1] = GetForLoopIndexA()
                        set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) ) + ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) )] = true
                        set udg_WARWAIT[( ( 11 * ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) ) + ( GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer()) - 1 ) )] = true
                        call TriggerExecute( gg_trg_War_Timer )
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005Func003001001)), "TRIGSTR_3066" )
                set udg_ALLYSETTING[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = false
            else
                if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005Func001C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005Func001Func005001001)), "TRIGSTR_3065" )
                    set udg_ALLYSETTING[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = false
                else
                    if ( Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Dip_War_Func001Func001Func005Func001Func001Func008001001)), "TRIGSTR_3064" )
                        set udg_ALLYSETTING[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = false

function Trig_Ally_Information_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_WHO = 1
    else
        if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001C() ) then
            set udg_WHO = 2
        else
            if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_WHO = 3
            else
                if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_WHO = 4
                else
                    if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_WHO = 5
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            set udg_WHO = 6
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                set udg_WHO = 7
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    set udg_WHO = 8
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        set udg_WHO = 9
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                            set udg_WHO = 10
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                set udg_WHO = 11
                                            else
                                                return
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call DisplayTextToForce( GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()), ( ( udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[udg_WHO] + "????." ) + "" ) )
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Ally_Information_Func003Func001C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce( GetForceOfPlayer(GetTriggerPlayer()), ( ( "" + ( "" + udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) ) + "? |cffccff00?|r????" ) )

        else
        endif

        else

 ?  function Trig_Init_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateMultiboardBJ( 3, 13, "TRIGSTR_4284" )
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 3
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 14
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), true, false )
            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), "" )
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 14
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, GetForLoopIndexA(), 10.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 13, ( "|c00FFFFFF" + ( "Time Elapsed" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, 1, ( "|c00FF0000" + ( "?" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, 1, ( "|c00ffab1e" + ( "??? + "|r" ) ) )
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 1
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 2
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 12
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + ( udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + "|r" ) ) )
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( true, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( false, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
    call EnableTrigger( gg_trg_Timer )
endfunction

        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, 13, ( "|c00FFFFFF" + ( ( I2S(udg_TimerMin) + ( ":" + ( "0" + I2S(udg_TimerSec) ) ) ) + "|r" ) ) )
    else
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, 13, ( "|c00FFFFFF" + ( ( I2S(udg_TimerMin) + ( ":" + I2S(udg_TimerSec) ) ) + "|r" ) ) )
    endif

function Trig_Set_Territory_Actions takes nothing returns nothing

    set udg_one[2] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(1), 'ncp2'))

    set udg_one[4] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(3), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[5] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(4), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[6] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(5), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[7] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(6), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[8] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(7), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[9] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(8), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[10] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(9), 'ncp2'))
    set udg_one[11] = CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(Player(10), 'ncp2'))
    set bj_forLoopBIndex = 2
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_one[GetConvertedPlayerId(ConvertedPlayer(( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )))]) + "|r" ) ) )

    endloop

function Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsInRectMatching(udg_rect[udg_interger], Condition(function Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001Func004Func004001001002))) >= 2 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Territory_Lose_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_interger = 0
    loop
        exitwhen udg_interger > 87
        if ( Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001C() ) then
            call TriggerSleepAction( 5.00 )
            if ( Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001Func004C() ) then
                call TriggerSleepAction( 1.00 )
                call DoNothing(  )
            else
                call SetUnitOwner( GroupPickRandomUnit(GetUnitsInRectMatching(udg_rect[udg_interger], Condition(function Trig_Territory_Lose_Func002Func001Func004Func003001001002))), Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), true )
            endif
        else
            call DoNothing(  )
        endif
        set udg_interger = udg_interger + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Territory_Lose takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Territory_Lose = CreateTrigger(  )
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ( gg_trg_Territory_Lose, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH )
    call TriggerAddCondition( gg_trg_Territory_Lose, Condition( function Trig_Territory_Lose_Conditions ) )
    call TriggerAddAction( gg_trg_Territory_Lose, function Trig_Territory_Lose_Actions )
endfunction

 ?  function Trig_Start_Turn_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( ( ( udg_one[GetForLoopIndexA()] * 100 ) * 1 ), ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER )
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( ( udg_one[GetForLoopIndexA()] * 25 ), ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call CreateMultiboardBJ( 3, 13, "TRIGSTR_4284" )
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 3
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 14
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), true, false )
            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), "" )
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 14
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, GetForLoopIndexA(), 10.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopBIndex = 2
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + ( udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + "|r" ) ) )
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_one[GetConvertedPlayerId(ConvertedPlayer(( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )))]) + "|r" ) ) )
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )]) + "|r" ) ) )
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 13, ( "|c00FFFFFF" + ( "Time Elapsed" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, 1, ( "|c00FF0000" + ( "?" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, 1, ( "|c00ffab1e" + ( "??? + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( true, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( false, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
    call PolledWait( 0.50 )
    call StartTimerBJ( udg_Turn, false, 89.50 )
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Start_Turn takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Start_Turn = CreateTrigger(  )
    call DisableTrigger( gg_trg_Start_Turn )
    call TriggerRegisterTimerExpireEventBJ( gg_trg_Start_Turn, udg_Turn )
    call TriggerAddAction( gg_trg_Start_Turn, function Trig_Start_Turn_Actions )
endfunction

 ?  function Trig_TimerSet_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateTimerDialogBJ( udg_Turn, "TRIGSTR_4286" )
    set udg_Timerwindows = GetLastCreatedTimerDialogBJ()
    call TimerDialogDisplayBJ( true, udg_Timerwindows )
    call StartTimerBJ( udg_Turn, false, 120.00 )
    call EnableTrigger( gg_trg_Start_Turn )
endfunction

        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, ( GetForLoopIndexA() + 1 ), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()]) + "|r" ) ) )

    call PolledWait( 0.50 )

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_All_Province_names takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_All_Province_names = CreateTrigger(  )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(0), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(1), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(2), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(3), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(4), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(5), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(6), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(7), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(8), true )
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerSelectionEventBJ( gg_trg_All_Province_names, Player(9), true )

function Trig_gold_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_gold_Func001Func001C() ) then
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( 18, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
            call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), 'ugol'), function Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func003A )
        else
            if ( Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( 24, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
                call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), 'ugol'), function Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func002A )
            else
                if ( Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003C() ) then
                    call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( 28, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
                    call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), 'ugol'), function Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func002A )
                else
                    if ( Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func003C() ) then
                        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( 31, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
                        call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), 'ugol'), function Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func003Func002A )
                    else
                        if ( Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func003Func003C() ) then
                            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( 31, ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
                            call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerAndTypeId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), 'ugol'), function Trig_gold_Func001Func001Func001Func003Func003Func003Func002A )
                        else
                            call DoNothing(  )
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

function Trig_Player_GG_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisplayTimedTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), 30, ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + "?(?? ????? ? ????? ???." ) )
    set udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = "?"
    set udg_Color[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = ""
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Player_GG_Func004Func001C() ) then
            call SetPlayerAllianceStateBJ( GetTriggerPlayer(), ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_ADVUNITS )
        else
            call DoNothing(  )
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call CreateMultiboardBJ( 3, 13, "TRIGSTR_4284" )
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 3
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 14
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), true, false )
            call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), GetForLoopIndexA(), GetForLoopIndexB(), "" )
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 14
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, GetForLoopIndexA(), 10.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, GetForLoopIndexA(), 2.50 )
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 13, ( "|c00FFFFFF" + ( "Time Elapsed" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, 1, ( "|c00FF0000" + ( "?" + "|r" ) ) )
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, 1, ( "|c00ffab1e" + ( "??? + "|r" ) ) )
    set bj_forLoopBIndex = 2
    set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + ( udg_PLAYER_NAMEC[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )] + "|r" ) ) )
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_one[GetConvertedPlayerId(ConvertedPlayer(( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )))]) + "|r" ) ) )
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ( GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 3, GetForLoopIndexB(), ( udg_Color[0] + ( I2S(udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[( GetForLoopIndexB() - 1 )]) + "|r" ) ) )
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
    endloop
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( true, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
    call MultiboardMinimizeBJ( false, GetLastCreatedMultiboard() )
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

function Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Func001C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Func001Func001C() ) then
            call UnitDamageTargetBJ( GetAttacker(), GetAttacker(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttacker()) * ( 20.00 / 100.00 ) ), ATTACK_TYPE_MELEE, DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL )
            call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Func001Func001Func002001001)), "TRIGSTR_3298" )
            if ( Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Func001Func001Func003001() ) then
                call KillUnit( GetAttacker() )
            else
                call DoNothing(  )
            endif
        else
            call KillUnit( GetAttacker() )
            call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Ally_is_your_side_stupid_Func001Func001Func005001001)), "TRIGSTR_3298" )
            call SetUnitLifeBJ( GetAttackedUnitBJ(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttackedUnitBJ()) + GetEventDamage() ) )
        endif
    else
        call DoNothing(  )
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002Func002C() ) then
            call CreateNUnitsAtLocFacingLocBJ( 3, 'n003', GetTriggerPlayer(), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()) )
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( -60, GetTriggerPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD )
            call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( -300, GetTriggerPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER )
        else
            call PolledWait( 0.02 )
            call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002Func002Func002001001)), "TRIGSTR_5523" )
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ( 'A02U', GetTriggerUnit() )
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ( 'A02U', GetTriggerUnit() )
        endif
    else
        if ( Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                call CreateNUnitsAtLocFacingLocBJ( 2, 'e003', GetTriggerPlayer(), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()) )
                call AdjustPlayerStateBJ( -370, GetTriggerPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER )
            else
                call PolledWait( 0.02 )
                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Supply_Depot_II_Func002Func001Func001Func002001001)), "TRIGSTR_5523" )
                call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ( 'A02W', GetTriggerUnit() )
                call UnitAddAbilityBJ( 'A02W', GetTriggerUnit() )
            endif
        else
        endif
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Middle_Age_I_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_Lumbermill[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 1
    else
        if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func001Func001C() ) then
            set udg_Blacksmith[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 1
        else
            if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_Church[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 1
            else
                if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_Armory[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 1
                else
                    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_Port[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 1
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    set udg_MiddleAge[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = ( ( ( udg_Lumbermill[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + udg_Blacksmith[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + udg_Church[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + ( udg_Armory[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + udg_Port[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) )
    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_I_Func003C() ) then
        call CreateNUnitsAtLocFacingLocBJ( 1, 'n00L', GetTriggerPlayer(), GetRectCenter(gg_rct________195), GetRectCenter(GetPlayableMapRect()) )
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_MiddleAge[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] < 3 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Middle_Age_II_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call PolledWait( 0.10 )
    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_Lumbermill[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 0
    else
        if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func002Func001C() ) then
            set udg_Blacksmith[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 0
        else
            if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_Church[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 0
            else
                if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_Armory[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 0
                else
                    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_Port[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = 0
                    else
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    set udg_MiddleAge[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] = ( ( ( udg_Lumbermill[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + udg_Blacksmith[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + udg_Church[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) + ( udg_Armory[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] + udg_Port[GetConvertedPlayerId(GetTriggerPlayer())] ) )
    if ( Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func004C() ) then
        call ForGroupBJ( GetUnitsOfPlayerMatching(GetTriggerPlayer(), Condition(function Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func004Func001001002)), function Trig_Middle_Age_II_Func004Func001A )
    else
    endif
endfunction

    if ( ( IsUnitOwnedByPlayer(GetUnitRallyUnit(GetTriggerUnit()), GetTriggerPlayer()) == true ) ) then
        return true
    endif

function Trig_Warp_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()) == Player(0) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( IsLocationVisibleToPlayer(GetUnitRallyPoint(GetTriggerUnit()), GetTriggerPlayer()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Warp_Func004C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not Trig_Warp_Func005C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Warp_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Distance = DistanceBetweenPoints(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), GetUnitRallyPoint(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call ShowUnitHide( GetTrainedUnit() )
    call PolledWait( ( udg_Distance / 1200.00 ) )
    call SetUnitPositionLoc( GetTrainedUnit(), GetUnitRallyPoint(GetTriggerUnit()) )
    call ShowUnitShow( GetTrainedUnit() )
endfunction

 ?  function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetFilterPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()) )
endfunction

function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func004001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetFilterPlayer() == GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()) )
endfunction

function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitType(GetAttacker(), UNIT_TYPE_STRUCTURE) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_ALLYSTATE[( ( 11 * ( GetConvertedPlayerId(ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB())) - 1 ) ) + ( GetForLoopIndexA() - 1 ) )] == 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetAttackedUnitBJ()) == ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexB()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()) == ConvertedPlayer(GetForLoopIndexA()) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001001001)), "TRIGSTR_4866" )
                    call UnitDamageTargetBJ( GetAttacker(), GetAttacker(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttacker()) * ( 5.00 / 100.00 ) ), ATTACK_TYPE_HERO, DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL )
                    call SetUnitLifeBJ( GetAttackedUnitBJ(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttackedUnitBJ()) + ( GetEventDamage() * ( 33.00 / 100.00 ) ) ) )
                else
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func004001001)), "TRIGSTR_4866" )
                    call UnitDamageTargetBJ( GetAttacker(), GetAttacker(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttacker()) * ( 10.00 / 100.00 ) ), ATTACK_TYPE_HERO, DAMAGE_TYPE_NORMAL )
                    call SetUnitLifeBJ( GetAttackedUnitBJ(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetAttackedUnitBJ()) + ( GetEventDamage() * ( 67.00 / 100.00 ) ) ) )
                endif
            else
                call DoNothing(  )
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA = CreateTrigger(  )
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ( gg_trg_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED )
    call TriggerAddAction( gg_trg_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA, function Trig_If_you_are_attacked_by_NA_Actions )
endfunction

    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Army_Elite_I_Func004Func001C() ) then
            if ( Trig_Army_Elite_I_Func004Func001Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Army_Elite_I_Func004Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] = ( udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] + 20 )
                else
                    set udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] = ( udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] + 4 )
                endif
            else
                set udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] = ( udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] + GetUnitLevel(GetDyingUnit()) )
            endif
        else
            if ( Trig_Army_Elite_I_Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
                set udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] = ( udg_PlayerUnitKillCount[GetForLoopIndexA()] + 1 )
            else
            endif
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

function Trig_Victory_I_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        set bj_forLoopBIndex = 1
        set bj_forLoopBIndexEnd = 11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopBIndex > bj_forLoopBIndexEnd
            if ( Trig_Victory_I_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                if ( Trig_Victory_I_Func002Func001Func001Func002C() ) then
                    set udg_Victory[GetForLoopIndexA()] = true
                    set udg_Victory[GetForLoopIndexB()] = true
                    call KillUnit( udg_Victoryunit[GetForLoopIndexA()] )
                    call KillUnit( udg_Victoryunit[GetForLoopIndexB()] )
                    call DisableTrigger( GetTriggeringTrigger() )
                else
                endif
            else
                if ( Trig_Victory_I_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_Victory[GetForLoopIndexA()] = true
                    call KillUnit( udg_Victoryunit[GetForLoopIndexA()] )
                    call DisableTrigger( GetTriggeringTrigger() )
                else
                endif
            endif
            set bj_forLoopBIndex = bj_forLoopBIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

function Trig_Message_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex = 1
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd = 12
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001C() ) then
            call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
        else
            if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
            else
                if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                else
                    if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Message_Func002Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        call DisplayTextToForce( GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_4926" )
                                    else
                                        call DoNothing(  )
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex = bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction
